<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Pefect! My husband and I stayed at the Omni on Aug 12-14. We were starting a ten day tour of the California coast and celebrating our five year anniversary. Our stay at the Omni was a perfect way to start this very special vacation! I had researched several BBs and hotels through Trip Advisor and decided on the Omni. We got our room for $135 for night one and $140 for night two - woo hoo! I had concerns of hearing outside noise in our room, the location being far away from things we'd want to see (we had never been to San Francisco), and the price of the mini bar. Here is what we found: We never heard any outside noise in our room. I am a very light sleeper, and no outside noise could be heard. The location was excellent! We could get to the Wharf in 20 minutes walking. The front desk will tell you how to avoid the hills. We only rode the cable cars once to say that we did it. We also rode the bus once to Haight Ashbury (Golden Gate Park) which was a very interesting trip. Our favorite section was the Italian District, lots of great places to eat and cool little bars! A very easy walk to/from the Omni. Don't hesitate to ask the front desk how to get places. They are very helpful! The Omni is located in the Financial District, so on the weekends the sidewalks aren't crowded. Finally, we never even opened the mini bar because of some of the reviews that we had read. There is a Trader Joe's close by where we purchased some wine and snacks. From reading a past review I joined (free) the Select Guest Program. This is a must! Just go to --- and fill out a quick form. We signed up just days before our trip. Because I signed up late, I emailed the Omni our guest number just to make sure that they had it on file. <Author>thehups
<Content>Our new #1 choice in San Francisco We've been happy with Omni properties previously and with the Phenomenal Fridays rate that we got, couldn't pass up trying this one. Our biggest regret is that we didn extend our weekend another day for more time here! From the time we arrived, the service was very personable and great. Check in took less than two minutes and upon arriving in our room, found a welcome note on the bed. The hotel was clean and even the smallest request was granted without asking. One example was when going out for our anniversary dinner, it was obvious we were dressed up for a special occasion. Instead of hailing us a cab as requested, he had a town car brought over to take us to dinner, complimentary. A very nice touch!My two recommendations to anyone staying here would be to sign up for Select Guest so at the very least you will bet a free juice and paper in the AM (and a big discount on a bagel/muffin). The other would be to verify your room size at check in. Traditionally, we have found corner rooms at the Omni to be of larger size so we try and request those. Here, it was an odd configuration (and a bit smaller) with part of a wall impeding the entry. Not a big deal since we probably only spent 4-5 hours in our room outside of sleeping but thought I would pass that along if.If you want a snack, there is a Subway across the street, a Mrs. Fields on the next block and a convenience store just around the corner. We bought drinks there and put them in the ice bucket; ready to drink when we got back from the day. They even added fresh ice when both when cleaning the room and at turndown.Location couldn't be better as we walked to Pier 39, Union Square and a very small hill (more of a grade) up to Grant Street and Chinatown.The bar was perfect for what we were looking for at the end of a long day, not a major party scene and not completely empty. We could carry on a conversation, hear the cable car as it went by and just enjoy the evening. Service was quick and the drinks were actually priced good for a hotel bar. Once again, very friendly and accommodating.I'll also have to second the Italian restaurant that the concierge recommended as it was perfect for a not too expensive dinner and was a walk of only 2-3 minutes. I'll also have to second the Italian restaurant that the concierge recommended as it was perfect for a not too expensive dinner and was a walk of only 2-3 minutes.I think the best compliment came from my wife when she said,  figured it would be nice but really had no idea it would be THIS nice.?Sure. getting a good rate helped but Il be back again and would still be just as happy paying full rate.

<Author>sune
<Content>Very good hotel I recently stayed 11 nights at the Omni San Francisco, first 8 nights May 30 ?June 7, and then another 3 nights June 16-19. I was very pleased with my stay at the Omni San Francisco. The staff was very friendly and helpful, and the 24 hours business service; which means free internet and free access to Microsoft word, Microsoft PowerPoint and even a possibility to make PDF files as well; was very valuable for me. The room was big (400 sq. ft.), clean, quiet, enough with TV channels, and the turndown service with ice and some chocolate in the evening was very nice. During my second stay I was happily surprised when I came back to my room since the manager had given me some nice chocolates as a gift since I was staying a second time at Omni San Francisco. Before I went to San Francisco I sign up for Omni Hotels Select guest service and it meant that you every day during your stay received some complimentary water, soft drinks, coffee or tea in the morning. I also had a complimentary late check out until 5 pm without any problems. When I gave some tip to the housekeepers they wrote a thank note. I was very pleased with the excellent service at Omni San Francisco. The Omni San Francisco is located in the financial district and is about 15 min walking to Union Square, and 35 min walk to fishermans wharf. Two blocks away up on a steep hill is Chinatown located with its many restaurants. There is a Walgreens one block away on Montgomery Street and it is a MacDonalds two blocks away as well. One block away on Kearney Street is a good Thai Restaurant (Bangkoks best). One of the reviews I read about Omni San Francisco said that it was boring and another review says that they should not stay at Omni again because the bar at Omni was not lively enough. If you are in San Francisco and is looking for a hotel there you should party, Omni may not be your kind of hotel. However, if you are like me, that you appreciate a hotel with friendly and helpful staff, excellent service, 24 hours free internet and business service; big, clean and quite rooms, good location, and close to many restaurants, you should consider staying at the Omni San Francisco. I highly recommend Omni San Francisco.

<Content>Regal Omni We enjoyed our stay at the Omni San Franciso. It's beautiful and service oriented. <Content>Nice digs, so-so service I stayed at the Omni in San Francisco this past weekend with a friend for just one night. It's beautifully and centrally located, just above Union Square, lovely hotel, everything seemed very clean and neat, and the staff was quite friendly. However, there were, in my opinion, three minor strikes against our particular stay. They all felt like problems that wouldn't typically happen, but maybe because there was somebody new  inexperienced on staff or something like that. Nevertheless:1) Reservations were under my friend's name. She called the day before to confirm. However, when she checked in, they told her that they had scheduled us to stay there on OCTOBER 11, not June 11. ??? Fortunately, she had the confirmation printout and they accommodated us immediately.2) My friend is highly allergic to animal products, and while confirming, she requested that they remove any  all down products from the room--synthetic pillows  blankets only. Well, when we settled in for the night, she started wheezing, tearing up, sneezing. (She wasn't even in bed yet--we were just sitting around, chatting  watching TV.) Sure enough, they hadn't removed the down pillows or duvet. She called, told them she was unhappy and had to request another blanket, which they brought up immediately. 3) We ordered hot chocolate, and it came up to us extremely... lukewarm.So, the service seemed good, but... some of this stuff shouldn't have happened in the first place. I'd stay there again, but if I had any special requests, I would follow through immediately. And I'd send the hot chocolate back.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>top notch hotel this hotel is worth the money we spent! we got a great deal through expedia. it's a little higher priced (more than $100 per night) but it was worth it! my review:1. we were upgraded to their signature room when we checked in. it's located in the higher floors with high thread count bed linens, an amazon shower head, great roomy room with luxurious features  design2. hotel itself is centrally located. if you don't mind walking about 4-5 blocks to: chinatown, nob hill  union square. you can also catch cable car which is right outside the entrance! cable car will take you to most major touristy sights in san fran, including fisherman's wharf.3. staff extremely helpful  friendly. the disadvantage of staying in this area is it's in the financial district so there are really no restaurants right outside the hotel. but the hotel's steakhouse (bob's) i understand is one of the best in the city. another thing is the parking! since it's downtown, parking is expensive or hard to find. if you park with the hotel, they'll charge you $40+ for valet!! there is a carpark building across the street which charge about $30 for 24 hour parking (or overnight). there's hardly any street parking. but if you're not driving, it won't be a problem. there are cabs readily available  of course the cable car.overall, omni is one of the best hotels i've stayed in =)

<Author>MisstheDogs
<Content>Pleasant Surprise I've almost come to expect substandard service from large hotel chains. Thus, I wasn't expecting much from my stay at the Omni in San Francisco and was pleasantly surprised at the high quality of the hotel and its service.The rooms are of adequate size and layed out in a manner that lets you either relax or work. There is a nice chair  ottoman and a good-sized desk. The TV rotates fully so that you can actually watch TV from the desk. The bed is comfortable and comes with an array of different styles of pillows. The bathroom is also of decent size and well-lit. There is free (i.e., no extra charge) high-speed internet service. The bathroom amenities are above average and include bath salts. There is nightly turndown service that includes, if necessary, fresh towels. For rainy days, there is an umbrella in the room and additional umbrellas are available at the front door. An array of newspapers (WSJ, USA Today, SF Chronicle) are available free of charge.The staff is unusually friendly and helpful. Check-in was a breeze. The front desk was never crowded, even though the hotel was. The concierge was helpful. Room service came promptly. Hotel staff greeted you when you arrived and left. Someone was always there to hold the door.The hotel is located a block from Chinatown and close to many good restaurants. The one negative was the elevator system. There are only 3 elevators for 17 floors and they are slow. Thus, during peak hours (7-9 a.m.), you must allow at least 10 minutes to get downstairs from an upper floor. Overall, however, the Omni gets high marks. I definitely recommend it, especially for business travelers.

<Author>babalootie
<Content>Stellar Service Lovely elegant room, not large, but nicely appointed with marble bath, minibar, free dsl. In-room CD player with a library at the front desk, could be more extensive, but hey. If you join the frequent stay club before you go, they will provide you with free morning beverages delivered to your room, reasonably priced room service (who ever heard of that!) and a newspaper. Parking is simply outrageous at $49 a night...I got rid of my rental car, and instead of returning it to the airport was able to drop it a few blocks away thanks to the quick intervention of the front desk personnel. The doormen, desk staff, housekeepers, all wonderful. I did have a nonfunctioning bathtub drain which wouldn't shut; a repairman was dispatched who said it was installed incorrectly and offered to change my room; after a call he kept working and pronounced it fixed. It wasn't fixed. Alas. The extraordinary amenity bath salts from Institute Swiss, down the drain...but that was the only hitch. All in all a wonderful stay in a well-located downtown property. A few blocks from the hot embarcadero center, and I even found a wine shop open Sunday at 7PM. You can't beat that.

<Author>Mrbigjerk
<Content>Solid Four Star Pick in Financial District While my wife and I normally stay at newer, trendier properties, the San Francisco Omni won us over with it's friendly, professional staff and convienent location. While our 17th story King room didn't offer the best views (think portholes for windows), the room itself was clean, quiet, well appointed, but not spectacular. Housekeeping did a fine job maintaining the room, but neglected to ensure a second roll of toilet paper was available. The mints offered during the evening turndown service were a nice touch.The hotel is more of a business hotel than resort property...no pools, spas, activity rooms, or even a small gift shop to be found. The business center did offer computers with complimentary high speed internet access, and the health club offered a variety of workout machines.Located midway between the Wharf and Union Square, and on the California street cable car line, the S.F. Omni is nicely located in the center of the financial district...seemingly hundreds of ATM's within a couple of blocks. Most attractions are easily within walking distance...but beware the hills, they can be a full blown cardio workout.Parking though is simply outrageous. $45 dollars a day puts the Omni well above neighboring garages...after the first night, we found cheaper near-by alternatives. Overall, the Omni staff impress you with their friendly demeanor and efficency...and although the property won't make you say wow, it's one of the better hotels we've ever stayed at. Well done!

<Author>Golfer919
<Content>Hard to Top This We stayed here on a Sunday night in March. Doorman was fantastic, and front desk staff were amazing. Its in the financial district, so that night there was hardly any street traffic. The next morning we walked to Union Square and its about a 7 block walk. Everytime we entered the lobby from the elevator or front door, we were always greeted cheerfully by name.This is a smaller hotel than the big monsters like the St.Francis, so there is not a gift shop, but a Bob's Steak and Chop House Restaurant. We were familiar with Bob's from Texas, but never ate there. We had planned to move the next day to the Monaco to be closer to Union Square, and noticed an immediate drop in service level. The rooms at the Omni are average size, and have a nice marble bathroom. They could use a separate shower. The room we had on the top floor, had a fruit basket and fax machine. Upon checkout, we were teased about leaving after just one night, and asked if they had done anything wrong. We replied Omni Service was great.During our stay in San Francisco, we went to the Ferry Market on Tue when they have local farmers kiosks set up. We also took a tour of the city with Great Pacific, a local small very nice tour company. Also drove one day over to Sausalito. Dined at Scoma's on the Wharf, Tadich Grill, Sam's Grill, and the Cheesecake Factory on Union Square. For lunch, there is a very busy In N Out Burger on the Wharf. Very good meals at all of them.The Cannery shops seemed to have fizzled since the 70's, and now the action has moved to Ghiardelli Square and Pier 39. We really loved our stay at the Omni, and talked about it on the flight home.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Superlative I was impressed by the service and the comfort that I found at the Omni - and I will be the first to admit that I am hard to please : ). This hotel had a knowledgeable, professional and friendly staff - their recommendations of a Chinese restaurant in nearby Chinatown or of a restaurant in close North Beach were spot-on when I made clear my price range and my expectations. The rooms had an understated elegance to them and there was considerable attention to detail - including a starched linen cloth at the foot of the bed for the slippers - a nice touch indeed. The location along the cable-car track put me at one end to Market Street and a connection near the top of Nob Hill brought me into either Union Square or Fisherman's Wharf in good time to enjoy the many things that San Francisco had to offer. Yet, being far enough away from the hectic activity of these places -- especially during this time of year -- made the hotel room a welcome refuge. Contrary to other reviews, I found the prices at both the restaurant and the lounge to be comparable and fair considering the location of the hotel in the Financial District and the level of service and quality provided. However, as I stated earlier, there are ample restaurants nearby from which you can choose. Finally, the use of a town car for a slightly higher fee than a taxi was an excellent touch. I travelled with 3 others who had a number of bags - and a Cadillac Escalade was ready at my time of booking to take our group to the airport. This truly is a superlative property. For the rate, it has to be the best value and the best comfort in San Francisco.

<Author>polodad
<Content>The SF Omni Hotel Was Wonderful! We live in a suburb of San Francisco metro area but because of a formal company Xmas party on Sat night 12/11/04 we decided to stay in the city and make a weekend out of it. I chose the Omni because of reputation, reviews, rating and price. Got it thru Hotwire, not inexpensive but a fabulous value. With Omni you can join their Select Guest Program before having stayed there. When in the program you receive room upgrades, amenities (continental breakfast, paper, bathrobes), and late checkout (5 pm). Prior to our arrival they upgraded us to a Premier View Room. The building is gorgeous. Lobby is dark wood and marble with beautiful furnishings. All of the hotel staff were professional, friendly, courteous and helpful. The room was on the 17th (top floor) and was huge. King size bed and a couch. Furnishings were similar to a very well done home. Bathroom was great also. The best feature, as promised, was the view. A panorama of Washington Square, San Francisco Bay, Angel Island and Sausalito. Wow!! We had just consumed half of the bottle of wine we had brought along when a bellman showed up with a welcome gift of champagne  chocolate dipped strawberries courtesy of the Select Guest Coordinator. Fantastic. Suggest parking at St. Mary's garage 1 block up Calif St with a weekend rate of a whopping $6 for 24 hours. Since the hotel was kind enough to furnish continental breakfast we only needed to split an omelet breakfast downstairs at the wonderful Bob's Chophouse. All in all, one of the best hotels I've ever stayed at and an amazing value on the weekend because it is in the financial district.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Love the Omni My S/O and I have stayed at the Omni 3 times now since July 2004, and have had a wonderful stay each time. It's very elegant, tasteful, and centrally located downtown at the corner of California  Montgomery.LocationGreat location right in the heart of the financial district. The cable cars are right out front, and the rail system is only several blocks away. We walked everywhere - Chinatown, Fisherman's Wharf (it's a long walk, but we like to walk), etc.StaffThe staff are very friendly and helpful. The housecleaning staff does a great job.RoomsThe rooms we have stayed in are nicely appointed, very clean, and quiet. We had a mini-bar (we took the things out and used the fridge for stuff we bought elsewhere). Plenty of room. High-speed internet access (complimentary), bathroom was decent size and very clean. The closet had extra pillows and blankets, a safe, and terry clothe robes awaiting us :) The bed was very comfortable, and the bedding was very clean.DiningWe ate elsewhere for each meal, but there is a full-service in-room dining menu available, and a restaurant in the lobby area of the hotel. It was a little too up-scale for us, but had great reviews from what we heard. Room service was a little expensive, so we stayed away from it. There were enough places within a few blocks to satisfy us. Exercise FacilityThe exercise room is very nice  spacious. There are 4 treadmills, each with it's own small TV and headphones - that was nice! There are also 3 ski-type machines, which had individual headphone sets to the 2 large TVs in the front of the room; 2 exercise bikes; a weight machine; and free-weights. Water bottles, apples, headphones, towels  newspapers were always available.Transportation to SFOThe Omni has a few house towncars available to take you to SFO if you want. If you want, you can reserve on at the front desk  charge it to your room. Cost was $57. For a slightly less amount, you can also just ask if a car is available when you are ready to go, and if it is, they will take you. The cost is $45. We took a cab from SFO to the Omni, and it was about $40, so the housecar price is pretty comparable, and it's a very nice car.OverallThis is a great hotel - we'd recommend it to anyone, and will stay there the next time we go to San Francisco.  
<Date>Oct 2, 2004

<Author>lunchinlewis
<Content>Excellent hotel with little gaffs We just spent 4 nights in this classy hotel. Without repeating all the deserving praise this hotel receives here, I'll bring up just a few little things that I thought could use some attention.Immediately after checkin we had to head out to meet friends at the Savoy for dinner. Having never been to San Fran, we strolled out the front door and asked the doormen how to get there. They didn't know. When we mentioned the intersection, they finally gave us good directions. The woman who checked us in also seemed a little unsure of procedures, but she may have been a new hire.Housekeeping was great, but slowly tailed off with each day. Little things like having to call down at night because the in-room coffee service was not properly restocked each night. But they delivered whatever we needed promptly, at all hours.I would think a hotel like this would have a removable shower nozzle. This one was mounted very high with little adjustment.They should consider more counter space in the living area, with amenities like kleenex. When the bathroom is occupied, you're pretty much on your own. A small dresser would fit nicely.We had a room on the 11th floor, on the front of the building. It was loud, lots of street noise at all hours. But typical of a city hotel. The curtains were superb at blocking the light, almost too good as it kept us in bed thinking it was earlier.But that's just nitpicking. I'd stay there again for sure.

<Author>WineTool
<Content>Great service, helpful staff We've stayed at the Omni twice, and both times the experience was very good. The rooms are nice and large - maybe not stylish, but comfortable, clean, and nicely decorated. What stands out at the Omni is the service. Check-in took all of 30 seconds, and housekeeping responded very quickly to our request for different sheets (it looked like there was some kind of grease that got on them). Everyone I talked to was helpful and knowledgeable, and, best of all, not too hip for their own goodMy only complaint, which I've seen from other guests as well here, is the price of drinks in the hotel bar. $9.50 for a Campari and soda is absurd, and $12.95 for a Grand Marnier (a single, mind you) is downright preposterous. I like to have a relaxing drink in the hotel lounge before bed, but not at those prices. It may be a small thing, but for me it makes the Omni experience above average instead uof excellent.

<Author>DrewInLA
<Content>Very Good But . . . The Omni is a very nice hotel with the usual features for top quality hotels -- but no pool. The kids were disappointed a little by that. The rooms are very nice, clean, well kept--but for two adults and two younger teenage children they were a little crowded. Included one desk and chair and one easy chair. Just fine for two, however. It's a good, well-run hotel, but with a few mild negatives.Good, helpful staff always, but so young. What happened to old, genteel hotel staff?!The two large beds we asked for turned out to be full size, not king or queen, so the two kids felt a little cramped. The room was very clean, the bathroom nice, but had a sliding door to fit the room. Closet had bathrobes, ironing board, iron, even an umbrella. Computer ports, big TV, all the usual. Our view was of the back of other buildings and office windows. In other words, no view. Our rate was about $180 but with city hotel tax, etc. we paid over $200 for each of three nights in early July. Parking for our rental car was $45 a day! Next time I'll find a nearby garage. St Mary's Garage only two blocks up California St. might be cheaper. There's only one restaurant in the hotel. Breakfasts were very nice, service attentive, but expensive. Fortunately, when we reserved and asked about their best rates the hotel gave us six free breakfast vouchers so one-and-a-half day's breakfasts were free. That saved quite a bit. Dinners would have been very expensive and were the meat and potatoes type, so we ate elsewhere.The lobby is very nice--marble, artwork, some chairs, etc., but not a good place to lounge like the Fairmont or other great old hotels. One caution is that this hotel is in the Financial District. This is not Union Square or other hotel areas. At night and on weekends it's pretty empty, no restaurants nearby, and coffee shops and delis only cater to the business crowd so they close very early (4:00 is typical). But Chinatown is only two uphill blocks away so that's nice. Summer in SF is very windy and chilly, so we battled winds every day. Take a windbreaker for sure. I'd stay at the Omni again for $200 or less. At higher rates, I'd expect a bigger room, a coffee shop, pool, more central location.

Really enjoyed the stay as the hotel was beautiful in general, and the room in particular. Furnishings were clean, elegant, and comfortable. Only downside was the staff were somewhat unknowledgeable about where to eat in San Francisco, and relied upon their computer system for information too much.

<Author>donnakat
<Content>The Omni was a great choice! From the time we checked in until the time we left we were treated like royalty. I reveiwed many hotels in San Francisco before making the reservations at Omni and was overwhelmed with the choices. I am very happy that I settled on the Omni. The rooms are large and well apointed. We joined the Omni Select Guest Progam (free) and received coffee, juice and newspaper every morning. The staff, even the bartender in the lounge were very helpful and friendly. They gave us great sight seeing tips. The front desk even got us tickets to the Giants game. The restaurants that they recommended were wonderful - try Rose Pistola or any cafe on Belden Alley.

<Author>Vegasdebut007
<Content>What a wonderful place to stay This was our first time in San Francisco and the first time we had stayed at an OMNI. The reviews on tripadvisor were excellent and the price we got on the internet was very good. We stayed from April 12 for 3 nights. From the outset our experience of San Francisco was great but the hotel made it a wondewrful stay. We were taken from the superbly decorated entrance hall to our good sized room by a young man who was informative and keen to share his city with visitors. The room was modern, well eqipped and absolutely pristine. The fittings were brand new and care has been taken to maintain such good order.We took the MUNI pass which gives unlimited travel on the cable cars busse etc and saw all the sites except for Alcatraz - we hadn't booked. In summing up we would recommend this OMNI to anyone. Remember to join the OMNI club before you travel. The OMNI is excellent value for money because of the location, keen polite staff, lovely modern pristine room, and the general attention to detail.
